Thanks for using Fredboat Music! To get started, join a voice channel and type `;;play <song name>`. I'll give you a list of 5 songs where you can choose one by typing `;;play <number>`.

Type `;;commands` for a list of commands you can use! Or go to <https://fredboat.com/docs> for a full review of what I can do. Type `;;help` for documentation, bot invite links, and an invite to the Fredboat Hangout Discord Server.

You can set up FredBoat to announce music as it plays and automatically resume when a user enters the channel with the `;;config` command.

I can speak your language, too! Type `;;language` to see a list of languages I can speak. It should look like this: `;;language en_US` but with your language code.

I have a built in permissions system you can use! Follow this link to learn more: <https://fredboat.com/docs/permissions>

>help rs


[25-Aug-20 01:29 AM] owo#0498

{Embed}
```>recent [username...]                   ```
Get user's most recent plays. Mode defaults to set default gamemode.

**[Options]**
username: username of the player.
Mode `(-m)`: 0 = std, 1 = taiko, 2 = ctb, 3 = mania
Server: -ripple, -gatari, -akatsuki, -official
Recent best `(-)`: Gets most recent score in top 100. `(no param)`
Specific Play `(-p)`: Get specific play number from recents. `(1-50)`
Specific Play `(-g)`: Get a completion graph of your play. Only if failed.
List `(-l)`: List 5 most recent plays.

**[Example]**
`>recent - Neo - -b`

>badge


[31-Aug-20 10:46 PM] owo#0498

{Embed}
```>badge                                                                ```
Do fancy things with badges.```give           Give a specific user a badge. Used
               mostly for unpurchaseable badges `(-1)`.
available      Get a list of available badges for
               server.                  
buy            Get a badge from repository.
link           Associate a role with a level. Only one
               link per badge.          
equip          Put a badge onto your profile. You must
               equip in server to which the badge
               belongs.                 
unlink         Delete a role/level association.
listlinks      List level/role associations.
add            Add a badge for your server. Limit 25
               per server `(so think about adding
               wisely)`.                 
delete         Delete a badge. Users with badge will
               still have it.           
```

```>recommend [options...]                 ```
Get a recommendation for a map. Ranges should follow `x1-x2` format.

**[Options]**
Stars `(-s)`: The target stars of your map. `(float/range)`
Approach Rate `(-ar)`: Target approach rate for recommended map. `(float/range)`
Overall Diff `(-od)`: Target overall diff for recommended map. `(float/range)`
HP `(-hp)`: Target HP for recommended map. `(float/range)`
Cricle Size `(-cs)`: Target cs for recommended map. `(float/range)`
PP `(-pp)`: Target fc pp for recommended map. `(float/range)`
Graph `(-g)`: Get a graph for the map that is recommended.
Farm Rating `(-f)`: How much of a farm map it is. `(1 `(hard)`-10 `(easy)`)`
Mods: Modes that you want to apply, no - needed. Use "any" for any/NM for no mod.

**[Example]**
`>recommend -pp 500 HDDT -ar 10.3 -g`

[08-Sep-20 12:01 PM] owo#0498

{Embed}
```>recent [username...]                   ```
Get user's most recent plays. Mode defaults to set default gamemode.

**[Options]**
username: username of the player.
Mode `(-m)`: 0 = std, 1 = taiko, 2 = ctb, 3 = mania
Server: -ripple, -gatari, -akatsuki, -official
Recent best `(-)`: Gets most recent score in top 100. `(no param)`
Specific Play `(-p)`: Get specific play number from recents. `(1-50)`
Specific Play `(-g)`: Get a completion graph of your play. Only if failed.
List `(-l)`: List 5 most recent plays.

**[Example]**
`>recent - Neo - -b`

[16-Sep-20 08:20 PM] owo#0498

{Embed}
```>recent [username...]                   ```
Get user's most recent plays. Mode defaults to set default gamemode.

**[Options]**
username: username of the player.
Mode `(-m)`: 0 = std, 1 = taiko, 2 = ctb, 3 = mania
Server: -ripple, -gatari, -akatsuki, -official
Recent best `(-)`: Gets most recent score in top 100. `(no param)`
Specific Play `(-p)`: Get specific play number from recents. `(1-50)`
Specific Play `(-g)`: Get a completion graph of your play. Only if failed.
List `(-l)`: List 5 most recent plays.

**[Example]**
`>recent - Neo - -b`

`>osutop - Neo -`

[25-Oct-20 01:35 AM] - Neo -#0727
Summary of the vmulti bug: it somehow stretches your monitor area to all monitors and essentially makes a ratio of whatever the setting used on your monitors when you load otd. So 1920x1080 setting loaded on a dual monitor setup that has 3840x1080 total area gets the area stretched and for every pixel you change on the stretched monitor area setting it changes a different amount when actually using the tablet. So for a horizontal two monitor setup it changes two pixels of width every one pixel changed. This bug also redoes itself every time otd is loaded. So if you set 960x1080 to half the area which would condense it to one monitor in the previous example it will take 960x1080 and stretch it across both monitors when otd is restarted. This ends up with the pixels multiplying by 4x width.

[26-Oct-20 04:13 AM] - Neo -#0727
**Which tablet driver should I get?**

There's tl;dr on the bottom, so go check if you don't wanna go though everything!

You might be struggling to choose which tablet driver to use, don't worry! This post will go through 3 kinds of tablet drivers and compare which one's better than the others.

**1st. OEM drivers**: OEM drivers, like Wacom/XP-Pen drivers, are not optimized for osu! experience. No, I'm not saying they're bad, it's just they lack customization options (e.g. Smoothing filters). They also have not-customizable software smoothing, which might be unhelpful. *Not really recommended*
    Pros:
    Cons:

**2nd. OpenTabletDriver (a.k.a. OTD)**: OTD is a not well-known 3rd party driver, but probably is the best tablet driver among this list. Updates are still getting released, It is VMulti less, and  it's cross platform software.  It also has plugins that lets you use all the functions in hawku and Devocub drivers, meaning you can get same experience as those two.
    Pros:
    Cons:

**3rd. VMulti based drivers**: Ah yes, the hawku/Devocub driver that we all know, are VMulti based drivers. They've been known for long time, are they still good?
Yes!...but also no. 
    Pros: 
    Cons:

tl;dr : OTD is the recommended driver. Also ping @- Neo - if you want support/extra questions!


- Multi monitor support of VMulti is poor.
- It has latency issue compared to VMulti less drivers like OTD, since VMulti takes more process.
Overall, although it is use by most people, it's currently outdated, old driver.

[26-Oct-20 03:30 PM] owo#0498

{Embed}
```>recommend [options...]                 ```
Get a recommendation for a map. Ranges should follow `x1-x2` format.

**[Options]**
Stars `(-s)`: The target stars of your map. `(float/range)`
Approach Rate `(-ar)`: Target approach rate for recommended map. `(float/range)`
Overall Diff `(-od)`: Target overall diff for recommended map. `(float/range)`
HP `(-hp)`: Target HP for recommended map. `(float/range)`
Cricle Size `(-cs)`: Target cs for recommended map. `(float/range)`
PP `(-pp)`: Target fc pp for recommended map. `(float/range)`
Graph `(-g)`: Get a graph for the map that is recommended.
Farm Rating `(-f)`: How much of a farm map it is. `(1 `(hard)`-10 `(easy)`)`
Mods: Modes that you want to apply, no - needed. Use "any" for any/NM for no mod.

**[Example]**
`>recommend -pp 500 HDDT -ar 10.3 -g`

definition_number: The definition number `(int)`

[28-Oct-20 11:27 AM] MEE6#4876

{Embed}
Moderator Plugin
`!ban [member] (optional reason)`
Bans a member from the server

`!tempban [member] [duration] (optional reason)`
Temporarily bans a member from the server

`!clear (optional member) (optional count)`
Clears messages in a particular channel

`!clear-all-infractions`
Remove all the infractions of everyone in the server

`!infractions [member]`
Displays how many infractions this member has

`!kick [member] (optional reason)`
Kicks a member from the server

`!mute [member] (optional reason)`
Mutes a member in the whole server

`!tempmute [member] [duration] (optional reason)`
Temporarily mutes a member in the server

`!role-info [role]`
Gets information about a role

`!server-info`
Gets information about your server

`!slowmode (optional timeout) (optional off)`
Enables/Disables slowmode in a channel

`!unban [member]`
Unbans a member

`!unmute [member]`
Unmutes a member

`!user-info (optional member)`
Gets information about a user

`!warn [member] (optional reason)`
Warns a member
https://images-ext-2.discordapp.net/external/RyBiRwUtq8VqdDb6Sm77J303UEziO55Ujqu8FaRCfQ4/https/i.imgur.com/JsgxK3Y.png

[17-Nov-20 08:27 AM] MEE6#4876

{Embed}
Music Plugin
`!add [search]`
Add a music to the queue

`!add-playlist [playlist_url]`
Adds a whole youtube playlist to the queue

`!clear-queue`
Clears the current queue

`!join`
Joins the user voice channel

`!leave`
Leaves current voice channel

`!np`
Display the current playing track

`!pause`
Pause the current playing song

`!play (optional search)`
Adds the song to the queue and plays it if the queue is empty

`!previous`
Plays the previous track

`!queue`
Display the current queue

`!replay`
Replays the current music

`!resume`
Resume playing the current song

`!search [search]`
Searches for a song that can be later added to the queue

`!seek [position]`
Change the current track's position

`!skip`
Skips to the next song in the queue
Page 1/2

{Reactions}

[25-Nov-20 03:44 PM] owo#0498

{Embed}
```>recent [username...]                   ```
Get user's most recent plays. Mode defaults to set default gamemode.

**[Options]**
username: username of the player.
Mode `(-m)`: 0 = std, 1 = taiko, 2 = ctb, 3 = mania
Server: -ripple, -gatari, -akatsuki, -official
Recent best `(-)`: Gets most recent score in top 100. `(no param)`
Specific Play `(-p)`: Get specific play number from recents. `(1-50)`
Specific Play `(-g)`: Get a completion graph of your play. Only if failed.
List `(-l)`: List 5 most recent plays.

**[Example]**
`>recent - Neo - -b`

[01-Dec-20 01:58 AM] MEE6#4876

{Embed}
Moderator Plugin
`!ban [member] (optional reason)`
Bans a member from the server

`!tempban [member] [duration] (optional reason)`
Temporarily bans a member from the server

`!clear (optional member) (optional count)`
Clears messages in a particular channel

`!clear-all-infractions`
Remove all the infractions of everyone in the server

`!infractions [member]`
Displays how many infractions this member has

`!kick [member] (optional reason)`
Kicks a member from the server

`!mute [member] (optional reason)`
Mutes a member in the whole server

`!tempmute [member] [duration] (optional reason)`
Temporarily mutes a member in the server

`!role-info [role]`
Gets information about a role

`!server-info`
Gets information about your server

`!slowmode (optional timeout) (optional off)`
Enables/Disables slowmode in a channel

`!unban [member]`
Unbans a member

`!unmute [member]`
Unmutes a member

`!user-info (optional member)`
Gets information about a user

`!warn [member] (optional reason)`
Warns a member

[20-Dec-20 08:20 PM] flowabot#5018

{Embed}
Commands
`!render`, `!frame`, `!fail`
Description
Render picture or gif of a beatmap at a specific time. Videos 10 seconds or longer are automatically rendered as mp4 video with audio and beatmap background.
Usage
```!render [beatmap url] [+mods] [AR8] [CS6] [preview/strains/aim/speed/fail] [20%] [mp4] [plain] [120fps] [mm:ss] [353x] [4s]```
Examples
```!render strains```Returns a gif of the hardest part on the last beatmap.

```!fail```Returns a gif of the part where the player failed on the last beatmap.

```!render 1:05```Returns an image of the last beatmap at 1 minute and 5 seconds.

```!render speed 10s 50%```Returns a 10 second video of the streamiest part on the last beatmap at half speed.

```!render 120fps 353x plain```Returns a 120fps video at 353 combo on the last beatmap without sound and black background.

[21-Apr-21 12:35 AM] - Neo -#0727
```    def construct(self):

        theta = ValueTracker(0)
        line1 = Line(ORIGIN,RIGHT*3,color=RED)
        line2 = Line(ORIGIN,RIGHT*3,color=GREEN)
        line3 = Line(line1.get_end(),line2.get_end())

        line2.add_updater(lambda x : x.rotate(theta.get_value(),about_point=ORIGIN))
        line3.add_updater(lambda x : x.become(
            Line(line1.get_end(),line2.get_end(),color=BLUE)
        ))

        arc = Arc(radius=3,start_angle=line1.get_angle(),angle=theta.get_value(),color=ORANGE)
        arc.add_updater(lambda x : x.become(Arc(radius=3,start_angle=line1.get_angle(),angle=theta.get_value(),color=ORANGE)))
        self.add(line1,line2,arc,line3)
        
        self.play(theta.animate.increment_value(PI*2),run_time=5)```

[06-May-21 11:34 AM] owo#0498

{Embed}
```>recent [username...]                   ```
Get user's most recent plays. Mode defaults to set default gamemode.

**[Options]**
Username: username of the player.
Server `(-{server name})`: >botinfo for list of supported servers. 
Recent best `(-b)`: Gets most recent score in top 100. `(no param)`
Graph `(-g)`: Get a completion graph of your play. Only if failed. `(no param)`
Play index `(-i)`: Get specific play number from recents. `(1-50)`
Image `(-im)`: Generates score image of play. `(no param)`
List `(-l)`: List 5 most recent plays. `(no param)`
Mode `(-m)` or `(-{mode})`: 0 = std, 1 = taiko, 2 = ctb, 3 = mania `(int or tag)`
Now Playing `(-np)`: Get currently playing. Must have discord presence enabled. `(no param)`
Page `(-p)`: Get another page of the list. `(int)`
Pass only `(-ps)`: Filter pass-only scores. `(no param)`
Search `(-?)`: Search by map name. Will grab first match. `(str)`
User `(-u)`: Ignore discord users with same username. `(no param)`

**[Example]**
`>recent - Neo - -b -ripple`

B= Number of BALLS

T= Number of TITS
G= Gayness.

G=(D+B)/(V+T)= Gayness Ratio.

1 man 1 woman = (1+2)/(1+2)=1= Heterosexual baseline (Vanilla)

No woman: G = N/0 = infinitely gay

No men: G = 0/N = 0 gayness.

MFF threesome: G = (1+2)/(2+4)= 0.5, Better than Vanilla

MMF threesome: G = (2+4)/(1+2) = 2, twice as gay as vanilla.

1 shemale solo: G = (1+2)/(0+2) = 1.5, Less gay then MMF, but more gay than vanilla.

[07-Apr-22 12:29 AM] - Neo -#0727
```py
file = open("KakaoTalk_20220406_2100_52_550_group.txt", 'r', encoding='utf8')

contents = file.readlines()

file.close()

content = list()

countdict = dict()

for i in contents:
    if(i[0]=="["):
        content.append(i)

laugh = "ㅋㅋ"


print("입력하세요.")
targets = input()

targets = targets[1:]

if (targets == "laugh"):
    targets = laugh



for target in targets:
    for line in content:
        name = line[1:line.index("]")]
        talk = line[line.index("]")+1:]
        talk = talk[talk.index("]")+2:]

        if(list(countdict.keys()).count(name)==0):
            countdict[name] = 0

        if(talk.find(target)!=-1):
            countdict[name] = countdict[name] + 1

print(countdict)
```

[07-Apr-22 08:37 PM] - Neo -#0727
```py
def analyze(keyword):
    file = open(r"C:\Users\ohmay\OneDrive\KHU\Grade1\Dasom\Kakao.txt", 'r', encoding='utf8')

    raw_data = file.readlines()

    file.close()

    data = list()

    countdict = dict()

    for i in raw_data:
        if(i[0]=="["):
            data.append(i)


    for target in keyword   :
        for line in data:
            name = line[1:line.index("]")]
            talk = line[line.index("]")+1:]
            talk = talk[talk.index("]")+2:]

            if(list(countdict.keys()).count(name)==0):
                countdict[name] = 0

            if(talk.find(target)!=-1):
                countdict[name] = countdict[name] + 1
    
    print(countdict)



if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("Input.")
    keyword = input()

    laugh = "ㅋㅋ"
    cry = "ㅠㅠ"
    swear = ['ㅂㅅ','ㅅㅂ','ㅈㄹ','ㅈㄴ']

    #keyword = keyword[1:]

    if (keyword == "laugh"):
        keyword = laugh
        analyze(keyword)

    elif (keyword == "cry"):
        keyword = cry
        analyze(keyword)

    elif (keyword == "swear"):
        for i in swear:
            keyword=i
            analyze(keyword)
    
    else:
        analyze(keyword)
```
